2. **Lobbying**: Companies would influence regulatory agencies and lawmakers to weaken environmental standards or delay enforcement. They would often employ experts in regulatory affairs to make the case for their interests.
3. **Cost-benefit analysis**: Businesses would argue that the costs of implementing regulations outweighed the benefits
